DDS

Document Divider System

Split & Create Job Descriptions

Split Existing Documents
Use this when you have a LARGE Word document containing multiple job descriptions (e.g., 46 JDs in one 92-page file). This tool will automatically split it into individual 2-page files, one for each job description.
How It Works
  • Scans for "Job Summary / Overview" followed by "Client - Job Title"
  • Extracts Job Code from the header table
  • Creates individual files: "Client - Job Title - Code.docx"
  • Each output file = exactly 2 pages with full formatting preserved

Drop your LARGE document here

Supported format: .docx (Max 50MB)

Processing your document...

Check browser console (F12) for detailed logs

Processing Complete!

0

Individual job descriptions created

Create NEW Job Description
Use this when you need to create a SINGLE new job description from scratch. Fill in the form below - the system will generate a properly formatted Word document matching your company template exactly.
Template Embedded!

Your company template is built into this system. Just fill in the job details and click "Create" - the result will match your exact format with logo, header table, and all formatting preserved perfectly!

Leave empty if not applicable
Each responsibility on a new line (bullets will be added automatically)
Each requirement on a new line (bullets will be added automatically)
